	OutputLine(NULL, "それを見て、慌てて部下の刑事たちが駆け寄ってきたが、彼女は気丈に『大丈夫』と手を上げて答え、首を振りながら速水刑事を伴ってパトカーの停車場所へと向かっていった。",
			NULL, "After seeing that, her team of detectives came running over, but she held up a hand to say \"I'm fine.\" Then she shook her head as she walked with Detective Hayami to the police car.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DrawScene("background/hata1_03", 1000 );
	ModDrawCharacter(3, 11, "sprite/oisi1_4_", "0", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 20, 200, TRUE );

//赤坂rvS08/13/321000462.「大石さん、これは一体、どういうことでしょう…？」
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#797d8a>赤坂</color>", NULL, "<color=#797d8a>Akasaka</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 13, "ps3/s08/13/321000462", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「大石さん、これは一体、どういうことでしょう…？」",
			NULL, "\"Ooishi-san, what the hell does all of this mean...?\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	ModDrawCharacter(3, 11, "sprite/oisi1_5_", "0", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 20, 200, TRUE );

//大石rvS08/11/321100357.「…どうですかねぇ。kvS08/11/321100358.赤坂さん、偶然だと思われますか？」
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#a59da9>大石</color>", NULL, "<color=#a59da9>Ooishi</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 11, "ps3/s08/11/321100357", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「…どうですかねぇ。",
			NULL, "\"...What, indeed.", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 11, "ps3/s08/11/321100358", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "赤坂さん、偶然だと思われますか？」",
			NULL, " Do you think it's a coincidence, Akasaka-san?\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//赤坂rvS08/13/321000463.「——」
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#797d8a>赤坂</color>", NULL, "<color=#797d8a>Akasaka</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 13, "ps3/s08/13/321000463", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「——」",
			NULL, "\"......\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//r私は、心の中で『こんな偶然があるのか！』と呻き声を漏らしていた。
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "私は、心の中で『こんな偶然があるのか！』と呻き声を漏らしていた。",
			NULL, "My heart was shouting \"There's no way this could be a coincidence!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//r大石さんには、私の心の呻きが聞こえていたのかも知れない。
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "大石さんには、私の心の呻きが聞こえていたのかも知れない。",
			NULL, "Maybe my heart was shouting loud enough that Ooishi-san could hear it.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//rだが、…どう答えればいい？
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "だが、…どう答えればいい？",
			NULL, "But still... how could I answer that?", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//rこれが偶然でないとしたら、『祟り』は現実にあるってことなのか？！
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "これが偶然でないとしたら、『祟り』は現実にあるってことなのか？！",
			NULL, "Would I be admitting the \"curse\" is real if I said it wasn't a coincidence?!", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//赤坂rvS08/13/321000464.「……ッ！！」
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#797d8a>赤坂</color>", NULL, "<color=#797d8a>Akasaka</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 13, "ps3/s08/13/321000464", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「……ッ！！」",
			NULL, "\"......!!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	PlaySE(3, "dageki", 256, 64);
	DrawBustshot(5, "white", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 30, 250, TRUE );
	FadeBustshot( 5, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 250, TRUE );
	ShakeScreen( 1, 15, 15, 2, 0, );
	Wait( 500 );

//rありえない…そんなこと、ありえるわけが…ッ！！
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "ありえない…そんなこと、ありえるわけが…ッ！！",
			NULL, "Impossible... That can't be possible...!!", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DisableWindow();
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 3000 );
	DrawBustshotWithFiltering(6, "cinema", "x", 1, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 1300, TRUE );
	DrawBustshot(7, "title02", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 26, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 2000 );
	DrawBustshot(5, "black", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	FadeBustshotWithFiltering( 7, "x", 1, FALSE, 0, 0, 1000, TRUE );
	DrawScene("black", 3000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

	DrawSceneWithMask("tips/kage003", "mask_1900", 7, 0, 300 );
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );

	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );
